  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b3c35c20-5f21-4e5c-b763-ecac23009d64'
      });

  <span id="freeText7242744108323757129" style="display:none">What does a kid do when it just won’t stop?<br /><br />Kevin Burns has had enough. Today, the bullying stops. Today, he has easy access to his father’s gun cabinet. Today, Kevin exacts his revenge.<br /><br />“You think I’m small? Maybe I am, but my gun is huge . . . Size does matter—the larger the gun, the larger the . . .” <br /><br />Jake Tracey’s phone buzzes. It’s a text from his brother, Kenny.<br /><br />Where are you?<br />English class.<br />Stay there. Someone has a gun. Lock the door.<br /><br />Bloomfield, Michigan, an affluent Detroit area suburb, is home to trial lawyer Zachary Blake. Other school districts envy Bloomfield, that is, until Kevin Burns commits shocking, all too familiar, acts of senseless violence. In the aftermath of the tragedy, everyone wonders ‘why?’. <br /><br />Zack Blake seeks answers, justice for the victims, including his own son. <br /><br />How does a kid get a cache of weapons?<br /><br />The sellers are politically powerful and cover up their role in the bloodbath. The 2nd Amendment protects them, doesn’t it? And President Ronald John, Zack’s old nemesis, is a friend. <br /><br />Can powerful evildoers be brought to justice? Can Zack expose a dark web weapons conspiracy and the abuse of absolute political power in court? <br /><br />How does a broken community heal?<br /><br />In Betrayal High, a Zachary Blake legal thriller, award-winning author/attorney Mark M. Bello answers these questions and more in this fifth installment of what many readers are calling the country’s best courtroom drama series. Prepare to get Betrayed . . . again.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3510330877" />
    <a title="Jin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/101938044-jin"><img alt="Jin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591712713p2/101938044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3510330877?book_show_action=true">Aug 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jin" href="/user/show/101938044-jin">Jin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3510330877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11669235597028610417">I have mixed feelings with this one. I really love reading legal thrillers and I still regularly read them (John Grisham has been one of my favourite authors since ever). <br/><br/>Some parts of the book definitely deserves 5 stars! I really loved the back and forth between Zachary Blake and Kenny or Barrington and his "entourage". I was also positively surprised by the epilogue because normally, they would just be boring, disclosing nothing new but this one wrapped up the story nicely. Furthermore, the b</span>
  <span id="freeText11669235597028610417" style="display:none">I have mixed feelings with this one. I really love reading legal thrillers and I still regularly read them (John Grisham has been one of my favourite authors since ever). <br /><br />Some parts of the book definitely deserves 5 stars! I really loved the back and forth between Zachary Blake and Kenny or Barrington and his "entourage". I was also positively surprised by the epilogue because normally, they would just be boring, disclosing nothing new but this one wrapped up the story nicely. Furthermore, the book was not just a regular disturbed-teenagers-shooting-school-disaster but it shed light on this terrible incident from different aspects. I loved the involvement of high level institutions and other parts without being too exaggerating, and another plus point: it didn't have this typical overwhelming American heroism which I really liked.<br /><br />But I had a hard time to get into the story in the beginning. I couldn't connect to Kenny, Jake and their mother at all, their discussions and dialogues felt artificial and distant. The writing for Kenny got better in the end but I felt that he was still too cagey compared to the other characters in the story. Whenever Kenny and his friends were not in a chapter, I really liked the writing so much more and I kind of feel sorry for that. <br /><br />Betrayal High is definitely a good read for all fans of a good, fast-paced legal thriller. I really enjoyed reading this and I'm looking forward to the next Zachary Blake case!<br /><br />**I received a free copy of this book via Making Connections for leaving an honest review. The thoughts and opinions expressed are my own.**</span>
  <a data-text-id="11669235597028610417" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18056096836353777299">This story could have been ripped from the news, and is more unnerving because of that. Is a mass school shooter just an evil kid, or is there something more involved. And how did a teenager get his hands on so much firepower. Grab yourself a big bowl of popcorn and settle in for an uncomfortable look into the underbelly of America in crisis. It shook me to even consider the possibility of this happening, and I think it will do the same for you. The author does a great job in showing the opposin</span>
  <span id="freeText18056096836353777299" style="display:none">This story could have been ripped from the news, and is more unnerving because of that. Is a mass school shooter just an evil kid, or is there something more involved. And how did a teenager get his hands on so much firepower. Grab yourself a big bowl of popcorn and settle in for an uncomfortable look into the underbelly of America in crisis. It shook me to even consider the possibility of this happening, and I think it will do the same for you. The author does a great job in showing the opposing sides, their legal arguments, their lack of remorse, and the greed involved. Great story!!<br /><br />I received an advance review copy for free, and I am leaving this review </span>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3500153874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8257583445880312365">This is my first time reading anything by this author, the cover picture and title caught my eye and then the blurb convinced me to read the book. This is an emotional subject and one that stirs up a lot of heated conversation and so I applaud the author for the way in which he addressed it. The plot and the characters all have great depth and emotion to them. I found this to be an awesome read.<br/><br/>I received a free copy of this book via Booksprout and am voluntarily leaving a review.</span>

<div id="review_3473440547" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3473440547" />
    <a title="Pallavi Sareen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22595830-pallavi-sareen"><img alt="Pallavi Sareen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473247887p2/22595830.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3473440547?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pallavi Sareen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pallavi Sareen" href="/user/show/22595830-pallavi-sareen">Pallavi Sareen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3473440547" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10454274648112350418">Even though I do love to read books on sensitive topics, it is very rare to come across such books especially in the fiction genre. The California shooting shook everyone to the core. Shooting, inside a school, a place which we often associate as a safe space for learning and personality development can be beyond traumatic. Mark M. Bello deals with this theme in his book Betrayal High. The book delves into the story of a school shooting in Michigan as told from different point of views to unders</span>
  <span id="freeText10454274648112350418" style="display:none">Even though I do love to read books on sensitive topics, it is very rare to come across such books especially in the fiction genre. The California shooting shook everyone to the core. Shooting, inside a school, a place which we often associate as a safe space for learning and personality development can be beyond traumatic. Mark M. Bello deals with this theme in his book Betrayal High. The book delves into the story of a school shooting in Michigan as told from different point of views to understand it. It goes beyond one-dimensional news stories, as the creative freedom of novels allows and creates the same atmosphere for the reader. <br /><br />I must say, it was terrifying. <br /><br />The initial chapters which introduced us to the various characters Kevin and Kenny had such different narration which immediately allowed the reader to understand the difference between a chaotic mind that had too much going on and a sane one. But I didn't like the fact that the book began immediately with the action. I would rather understand the characters beforehand and get a glimpse of the circumstances that led up to it. But what it does deal with is the aftermath, which is no less consequential. The trauma that such an incident leaves on the mind of everyone, even the ones not directly impacted is immeasurable. I saw Kenny struggle with his mental health despite being the hero of the situation and it felt so realistic. <br /><br /><i>“Kevin did not believe he was going to survive the shooting, did he?”<br />“No, he didn’t. He was shocked he survived. He planned to use a homemade bomb and two powerful automatic weapons to kill as many ‘bullies,’ as he refers to his victims, as he could. </i><br /><br />The legal battle is all the more exhausting to read, as they are exhausting to experience but at no point in the book did I feel like it wasn't worth it. Given the experience I had, I would love to read more book by Mark. So, I would definitely recommend picking this up. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10454274648112350418" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3444244171" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3444244171" />
    <a title="Reader Views" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48888810-reader-views"><img alt="Reader Views" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600777637p2/48888810.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3444244171?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reader Views" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reader Views" href="/user/show/48888810-reader-views">Reader Views</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3444244171" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6811852270268252904">“Betrayal High” is the latest book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller series by Mark M. Bello. The series engages readers in current issues relevant to social justice in America. “Betrayal High” tackles bullying, school shootings, and the ongoing political debate around the Second Amendment of the Constitution. <br/><br/>Kevin Burns seeks justice and revenge as the result of relentless physical and emotional abuse by his school peers. His retribution leaves several students and one teacher dead, with num</span>
  <span id="freeText6811852270268252904" style="display:none">“Betrayal High” is the latest book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller series by Mark M. Bello. The series engages readers in current issues relevant to social justice in America. “Betrayal High” tackles bullying, school shootings, and the ongoing political debate around the Second Amendment of the Constitution. <br /><br />Kevin Burns seeks justice and revenge as the result of relentless physical and emotional abuse by his school peers. His retribution leaves several students and one teacher dead, with numerous others critically injured. Kenny Tracey, a fellow schoolmate, is shot in the leg while trying to stop Kevin before he does any more harm. Did I mention, Kenny is trial lawyer Zachary Blake’s son? Zach handles the civil cases for the families of the victims – cases against Kevin’s family, the school system and a powerful gun manufacturer, Barrington Arms. Zach soon discovers foul play reaching the highest political offices of our country in an exciting courtroom drama you will not be able to put down once you start reading.<br /><br />There are so many impressive things to say about “Betrayal High.” First, the storyline is compelling and heart-wrenching. There are no winners in this scenario, but a series of devastating circumstances leading many to their breaking points. Though a fictional tale, the harsh realities of life in this 21st century really hits readers with tough, thought-provoking, soul-searching questions. What do we do about the ever-increasing instances of bullying? How do we keep guns from getting into the hands of children? How many school shootings do we have to incur as a society before people in power do the right thing? What does the Second Amendment have to do with weapons of mass destruction? When are we going to hold gun manufacturers, the NRA, and politicians to task? Whichever side of the coin you are on with any of these issues, “Betrayal High” has “food for thought” to offer everyone, through its candid, brutally honest message. The writing is brilliant and leaves the reader thirsty for more. I got so worked up while reading I wanted to highlight just about every sentence to go back to and contemplate at a later date. <br /><br />The characters are equally impactful. Their thoughts, actions, motivations – every character trait provides genuine, well-rounded development. With Kevin for example, you experience the full gamut of emotions. My heart ached for him when I learned the extent of the abuse he suffered, I experienced fear as he went on his shooting spree, was angry at him for taking matters into his own hands and finally, felt sorry for him as he faced the consequences of his actions. One of his quotes will stay with me for some time: “Prison provides me a safer environment than my community school ever did. How is this possible?” We have truly failed our children when they feel safer in prison than at home or at school.<br /><br />Kenny Tracey is another character that leaves an inspirational imprint on readers. This young man is a humble hero and wants to get guns out of the hands of people like Kevin. He starts an organization of young first-time voters giving politicians the option of doing the right thing or be voted out of office in the next election. His determination and strength in the face of adversity provides hope for the future. He says, “We’re kids. We don’t have all the answers, but sometimes we feel like we’re the only adults in the room.” Touché, Kenny. Touché. <br /><br />I loved everything about “Betrayal High” and highly recommend it to fans of legal and courtroom drama depicting current and relevant societal issues. I can’t wait to get my hands on the rest of the Zachary Blake series by Mark M. Bello! Well done!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6811852270268252904" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16676061242344436583">Zachery Blake is back. This time, he plays second fiddle to his oldest son, Kenny. Kenny and Jake, the younger son, are both in high school. High school, for most people, is not the funnest place to be at times. <br/><br/><br/>For their friend, Kevin, high school was akin to hell on earth. One fine day, Kevin decides that enough is enough and he is going to a little housekeeping. After a little training, he heads to school and kills nine people. Kevin's plan is rather interrupted when Kenny makes his move, get</span>
  <span id="freeText16676061242344436583" style="display:none">Zachery Blake is back. This time, he plays second fiddle to his oldest son, Kenny. Kenny and Jake, the younger son, are both in high school. High school, for most people, is not the funnest place to be at times. <br /><br /><br />For their friend, Kevin, high school was akin to hell on earth. One fine day, Kevin decides that enough is enough and he is going to a little housekeeping. After a little training, he heads to school and kills nine people. Kevin's plan is rather interrupted when Kenny makes his move, getting shot in the process. This kind of changes the end result and Kevin ends up in jail.<br /><br /><br />Zachery Blake then takes centre stage as he proceeds to prosecute Kevin for his conduct. This is only the first layer to peel aside. Zach also intends to prosecute the gun company as well. Only when he begins to dig deeper does he realise how deep the rabbit hole really goes. It also exposes him and his family to some very dangerous and motivated enemies who would like to clean up a few loose ends. <br /><br /><br />Mr. Bello, in his fifth Zachery Blake novel, delivers a wonderful combination of high school activism and danger, political intrigue and courtroom drama. The story is well conceived, imbued with reality and carries through to a satisfying conclusion. It is sadly rather relevant in today's day and age. At least in this story, you know justice will prevail in the end. <br /><br /><br />I am volunteering a review for the benefit of others."</span>

<div id="review_3449817805" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3449817805" />
    <a title="Kimberly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8091824-kimberly"><img alt="Kimberly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504545322p2/8091824.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3449817805?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kimberly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kimberly" href="/user/show/8091824-kimberly">Kimberly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/44597074-betrayal-high">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3449817805" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1883613291668052556">Betrayal High by Mark M. Bello is the 5th in the Zach Blake series. While I have not read the first 4, I did not have any issues reading this one as a stand alone. A young man living with parents that pay no attention to him, a school where he doesn't fit in, and tormented by bullies. All leading to a school shooting that could have possibly been avoid if someone just cared enough. I enjoyed reading this book, although it was less about the high school shooting (maybe about 1/3 of the book) and </span>
  <span id="freeText1883613291668052556" style="display:none">Betrayal High by Mark M. Bello is the 5th in the Zach Blake series. While I have not read the first 4, I did not have any issues reading this one as a stand alone. A young man living with parents that pay no attention to him, a school where he doesn't fit in, and tormented by bullies. All leading to a school shooting that could have possibly been avoid if someone just cared enough. I enjoyed reading this book, although it was less about the high school shooting (maybe about 1/3 of the book) and more about gun laws and going after the gun company and other bad people. I also found 2 new quotes that I love. I am definitely going to have catch up with the series, and am looking forward to the next one. "There is no love without forgiveness and there is no forgiveness without love." - Bryant McGill "When you hold resentment toward another, you are bound to that person or condition by an emotional link that is far stronger than steel. Forgiveness is the only way to dissolve that link and get free." - Catherine Ponder Thank you to BookSirens for the free digital ARC in exchange for an honest and voluntary review. All opinions are my own.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1883613291668052556" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3473978138?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jana" href="/user/show/1752810-jana">Jana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3473978138" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17596455734917095571">Mark M. Bello chose a current topic. But what is new is that he wove a thrilling story around it.<br/><br/>This novel deals with such an important, terrible and current topic. The book combines U.S. American history with current politics - although the name of the president is changed. I could see parallels to the school shooting in Parkland, Florida in 2018 and the movements in its aftermath. The book deals well with all parties involved and shows why there are regular school shootings in the U.S., esp. </span>
  <span id="freeText17596455734917095571" style="display:none">Mark M. Bello chose a current topic. But what is new is that he wove a thrilling story around it.<br /><br />This novel deals with such an important, terrible and current topic. The book combines U.S. American history with current politics - although the name of the president is changed. I could see parallels to the school shooting in Parkland, Florida in 2018 and the movements in its aftermath. The book deals well with all parties involved and shows why there are regular school shootings in the U.S., esp. in contrast to pretty much all other countries. The story succeeds in building up suspense through the personal points of views of the protagonists. It is this constant change of perspective that gives an insight into what all parties think - the shooter, the victims, the protesters, the gun lobby ... and it shows that not everything is black and white.<br /><br />The one thing I didn't like was that the whole story is narrated in present tense. This might be personal preference, but I found it weird and it prevented me from a very good reading experience.<br /><br />The novel is part of a series. Although I do not know the other parts, this was not a problem for me at all to understand everything that is going on.<br /><br />I recommend this book to everyone who wants to engage more with the topics of U.S. gun laws and school shootings. Esp. high school students can learn a lot through this fictional story and it might be easier to start with a novel.<br /><br />I received a free copy of this book via Booksprout and am voluntarily leaving a review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17596455734917095571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3435870125" />
    <a title="John" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/83754729-john"><img alt="John" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3435870125?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="John" class="user" itemprop="url" name="John" href="/user/show/83754729-john">John</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3435870125" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15780448148276929018">I just finished this book, the 5th story in the Zach Blake series. As in all of his other books, this story will grab you right away. The case involves two subjects which intersect in this story: Gun Violence and Bullying.<br/><br/>Zach gets involved with the case of a school shooting because his son Kenny was injured while attempting to stop future killings. This case really has 2 parts, one criminal and one civil. The criminal cause is well done and presents a clear rationale by Kevin the shooter why he</span>
  <span id="freeText15780448148276929018" style="display:none">I just finished this book, the 5th story in the Zach Blake series. As in all of his other books, this story will grab you right away. The case involves two subjects which intersect in this story: Gun Violence and Bullying.<br /><br />Zach gets involved with the case of a school shooting because his son Kenny was injured while attempting to stop future killings. This case really has 2 parts, one criminal and one civil. The criminal cause is well done and presents a clear rationale by Kevin the shooter why he did what he did. The interaction between Keven and his attorney Charlie, was one where Kevin asserted his rights and objected to the defense that Charlie wanted to use. Kevin wanted to get his message across to the public which he was able to do in the end.<br /><br />The 2nd case which was Civil had Zach representing all of the parties that were injured in the shooting. Zach suit was filed against the shooter, his parents and in addition to the School System and the Gun Dealers and Manufactures of the weapons involved. It was quite interesting to watch Zach work through the preliminaries taking depositions from the various individuals involved. It also displayed the type of individuals who supported Zach in gather all the background elements that would assist him with his questioning. This group was really exceptional in ferreting out exactly who the responsible parties were for the attempted murder of Zach's son Kenny. This brought a entirely new complexion to the case and showed how far individuals were willing to go to protect their illegal business activities.<br /><br />In order for you to find out exactly what the attempted murder incident involved and how Zach was able to settle his cases, then you must read this book. You won't be disappointed. In addition you will get a snippet of Mark's next book in the series to whet your appetite.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15780448148276929018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3434089835" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6095053601510244430">Betrayal High is the fifth book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thrillers, and Mark M. Bello again writes about topics that hit close to home. Kenny Tracey faces someone more harmful than the priest that abused him, but a fellow student who’s had enough and settles the school bullying with firearms. Out of fear for his son and a call for justice, Zack Blake takes on the big boys. Clare Gibson from the FBI and the Private Investigator Micah Love is hunting for pieces to the puzzle of who is involved i</span>
  <span id="freeText6095053601510244430" style="display:none">Betrayal High is the fifth book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thrillers, and Mark M. Bello again writes about topics that hit close to home. Kenny Tracey faces someone more harmful than the priest that abused him, but a fellow student who’s had enough and settles the school bullying with firearms. Out of fear for his son and a call for justice, Zack Blake takes on the big boys. Clare Gibson from the FBI and the Private Investigator Micah Love is hunting for pieces to the puzzle of who is involved in a murder. Will they find the clues needed to discover who was behind hiring the assassin who had Kenny in his cross hairs?<br /> <br />I love reading Mark M. Bello’s novels. He isn’t afraid to hit subjects that are uncomfortable. I don’t always like the stand that Zack takes. In this novel, I wished the side effects of bullying and neglect were pushed more, but that wasn’t the point of this novel. Overall, you will not find a legal thriller that is more intense and professional than by Bello. I am anticipating the next in this series, Supreme Betrayal.  </span>

  <span id="freeText13661511238396120177" style="display:none">Betrayal High by Mark M. Bello is the 5th in the Zach Blake series. <span id="freeTextContainer12729100040695932044">Kenny Tracey finds himself in the spotlight once again when a fellow classmate Kevin Burns walks into their high school and shoots and kills nine students and teachers and injured many more to include Kenny. Kenny was shot while stopping Kevin before he could get to his AK47. Kenny stepdad, Zack Blake will stop at nothing to find justice and change the rules about gun safety. Has Mr. Blake finally picked a battle he can not win and as he takes on the whole lot to include changing laws, banning g</span>
  <span id="freeText12729100040695932044" style="display:none">Kenny Tracey finds himself in the spotlight once again when a fellow classmate Kevin Burns walks into their high school and shoots and kills nine students and teachers and injured many more to include Kenny. Kenny was shot while stopping Kevin before he could get to his AK47. Kenny stepdad, Zack Blake will stop at nothing to find justice and change the rules about gun safety. Has Mr. Blake finally picked a battle he can not win and as he takes on the whole lot to include changing laws, banning guns, and the NRA.<br /><br />Mark M. Bello has hit it out of the park with his latest legal thriller Betrayal HIgh. I honestly had me in the first chapter and the face he allowed the character, Kevin, to survive the stand-off at the school as a complete bonus. You will find this to be easy to read the book, but it does cover some very hard truths. The fact he covers the death of children, school shootings, gun control, and the law in the first four chapters lets you know this is an emotionally charged book and is not for children. I did find parts of the story hard to read. The writing is well done and I can say nothing negative of the story-line. I just found myself crying a lot because of the emotional connection you feel for the characters. I actually even felt for the shooter Kevin,  everyone could see needed help and was offered none by anyone. A good book would be enjoyed by fellow legal thriller fans. Like I said before not an all age definitely adult level.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer4297832072300054232">We cannot blame a person for a mass shooting. The whole community and the country need to take responsibility when one occurs. This is portrayed in Betrayal High. From this book I read about stories on how each and everyone who were involved in the mass shooting were trying their best to not take the blame and would do anything to blame others. No doubt that Betrayal High is fiction, but the author wrote it like it was a documentary based on true events. It was both entertaining and informative </span>
  <span id="freeText4297832072300054232" style="display:none">We cannot blame a person for a mass shooting. The whole community and the country need to take responsibility when one occurs. This is portrayed in Betrayal High. From this book I read about stories on how each and everyone who were involved in the mass shooting were trying their best to not take the blame and would do anything to blame others. No doubt that Betrayal High is fiction, but the author wrote it like it was a documentary based on true events. It was both entertaining and informative for me as I am from Malaysia. Owning a personal gun is illegal here. So there are near to zero mass shootings in schools. From this book I learned a lot about how a country takes mass shootings as a big problem or not. They relate it to mental illnesses. As a person with mental illnesses I can understand why these two are related. It is like a suicidal person with access to loads of psychiatric meds. Those meds are like weapons. The difference is that the meds would only harm the suicidal person but the weapons kill others. I could see how the company that manufactured the weapons, the school , the parents of the students who died, the parents of the shooter , the shooter’s father ...(the list goes on) are fighting for their rights and also discussing on how to tackle the issues in the book. It saddens me when I read how some of them can be very blunt and selfish. Bullying was also mentioned in the book. It could lead to mental health issues then later to a mass shooting. <br />Kevin , the shooter has a lot of reasons to be angry which lead him to do what he did. This shows clearly that mental health is extreamely important especially in the 21st Century where everyone is judged no matter who they are. Being judged is extreamely painful and exhausting when one is just a teenager like Kevin - the odd one out! </span>

<div id="review_3473458691" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3473458691" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3473458691?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3473458691" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2119217553514773729">‘You think I’m small? Maybe I am, but my gun is huge.’<br/><br/>Michigan author Mark M. Bello is an attorney and a justice advocate, having earned his BA in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree form Thomas M. Cooley Law School. He spent forty years in the courtroom with high profile legal cases, and now offers his knowledge on his website Legal Examiner and Injury Board writing posts about safety, fairness and justice in the civil justice system. Mark consolidates his experiences </span>
  <span id="freeText2119217553514773729" style="display:none">‘You think I’m small? Maybe I am, but my gun is huge.’<br /><br />Michigan author Mark M. Bello is an attorney and a justice advocate, having earned his BA in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree form Thomas M. Cooley Law School. He spent forty years in the courtroom with high profile legal cases, and now offers his knowledge on his website Legal Examiner and Injury Board writing posts about safety, fairness and justice in the civil justice system. Mark consolidates his experiences in this series of novels – THE ZACHARY BLAKE LEGAL THRILLERS, of which BETRAYAL HIGH is Book 5.<br /><br />One reason Mark M Bello’s legal thriller series is so absorbing is the manner in which he draws parallels to contemporary controversies. In this series Bello has tackled the Church and clergy sexual abuse, white supremacists and the President of the US, law enforcement, racism, and now gun control and school shootings. <br /><br />By now, those who follow the Zachary Blake legal thrillers know the primary characters and the unique mode of communicating a story line that make these books so memorable: the need for introductions is less important, but Bello adds new personnel in this volume and in doing so stirs even more reflective thoughts! <br /><br />The synopsis is a fine guide for this fast paced story – ‘Bloomfield, Michigan, an affluent Detroit area suburb, is home to trial lawyer Zachary Blake. Other school districts envy Bloomfield, that is, until Kevin Burns commits shocking, all too familiar, acts of senseless violence. In the aftermath of the tragedy, everyone wonders ‘why?’. Zack Blake seeks answers, justice for the victims, including his own son. How does a kid get a cache of weapons? The sellers are politically powerful and cover up their role in the bloodbath. The 2nd Amendment protects them, doesn’t it? And President Ronald John, Zack’s old nemesis, is a friend. Can powerful evildoers be brought to justice? Can Zack expose a dark web weapons conspiracy and the abuse of absolute political power in court? How does a broken community heal?’ And once again the story rings true, especially in view of contemporary news.<br /><br />After reading the first four volumes, the central character Zachary Blake is now a substantial legal hero, and the manner in which master craftsman Bello manipulates his character’s movement and development is a witness to both the depth of his legal knowledge and his eloquent prose. The language is appropriate for each character, and the manner in which the multiple characters interweave is mesmerizing. This legal thriller series is of the first caliber! Highly recommended. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2119217553514773729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3494503078" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3494503078" />
    <a title="Mrs. Varela " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2430315-mrs-varela"><img alt="Mrs. Varela " src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3494503078?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mrs. Varela " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mrs. Varela " href="/user/show/2430315-mrs-varela">Mrs. Varela </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3494503078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8685806159093772854">Betrayal High is Mark M. Bello’s fifth book in his Zachary Blake Betrayal series. The opening of the story dives right into the mind of a bullied high school student who has had enough. Kevin Burns has decided to end the bullying once and for all at any cost. The day he enters his high school armed and ready to kill using guns from his father’s gun cabinet has a lasting impact on the residents of Bloomfield, Michigan. <br/><br/>Evil thoughts are ruling Kevin’s mind as he shoots his bullies and others who </span>
  <span id="freeText8685806159093772854" style="display:none">Betrayal High is Mark M. Bello’s fifth book in his Zachary Blake Betrayal series. The opening of the story dives right into the mind of a bullied high school student who has had enough. Kevin Burns has decided to end the bullying once and for all at any cost. The day he enters his high school armed and ready to kill using guns from his father’s gun cabinet has a lasting impact on the residents of Bloomfield, Michigan. <br /><br />Evil thoughts are ruling Kevin’s mind as he shoots his bullies and others who just happen to be in his pathway. Zachary Blake’s two stepsons attend the same high school and are in separate areas of the building as Kevin commits his crime. The oldest son, Kenny is shot just before law enforcement arrives. When Zach and the boys’ mother get the news, Zach becomes angry and the boy’s mother is distraught. Quickly going into lawyer mode, Zachary Blake wants answers. While all Kevin really wants is to teach people about how much bullying hurts emotionally and physically. <br /><br />Civil justice attorney Zachary Blake is soon engaged to represent Kenny and the families of the people Kevin killed and injured with a major lawsuit against the school department, the gun manufacturer, gun dealers, and Kevin’s parents for their neglect. As more details emerge events occur that reveal pure evil from characters who are greedy, narcissistic, and powerful that will go to no end to hide their misdeeds including the fictional president, Ronald John.<br /><br />As always, Bello reflects on real events in his stories making them relatable and thought-provoking. This story also becomes a testament to the younger generation becoming involved in change for the better good of this country. When you finish reading Betrayal High, I guarantee that you will be looking forward to reading the sixth book in this series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8685806159093772854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer18402190699658502900">Betrayal High is the fifth book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thrillers, and Mark M. Bello again writes about topics that hit close to home. Kenny Tracey faces someone more harmful than the priest that abused him, but a fellow student who’s had enough and settles the school bullying with firearms. Out of fear for his son and a call for justice, Zack Blake takes on the big boys. Clare Gibson from the FBI and the Private Investigator Micah Love is hunting for pieces to the puzzle of who is involved i</span>
  <span id="freeText18402190699658502900" style="display:none">Betrayal High is the fifth book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thrillers, and Mark M. Bello again writes about topics that hit close to home. Kenny Tracey faces someone more harmful than the priest that abused him, but a fellow student who’s had enough and settles the school bullying with firearms. Out of fear for his son and a call for justice, Zack Blake takes on the big boys. Clare Gibson from the FBI and the Private Investigator Micah Love is hunting for pieces to the puzzle of who is involved in a murder. Will they find the clues needed to discover who was behind hiring the assassin who had Kenny in his cross hairs?<br /> <br />I love reading Mark M. Bello’s novels. He isn’t afraid to hit subjects that are uncomfortable. I don’t always like the stand that Zack takes. In this novel, I wished the side effects of bullying and neglect were pushed more, but that wasn’t the point of this novel. Overall, you will not find a legal thriller that is more intense and professional than by Bello. I am anticipating the next in this series, Supreme Betrayal.  </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17220800217973229843">I am putting a disclaimer on this book that it could potentially contain triggers, especially for those folks who have been bullied. I think this book should be recommended reading for young people. This book tackles a big topic - that of bullying. It tells the story from the perspective of a young man who was bullied and the consequences his "abuse" had on his life, and touches on the relationship he had with his family. It tells the story of a strong family relationship, from the perspective o</span>
  <span id="freeText17220800217973229843" style="display:none">I am putting a disclaimer on this book that it could potentially contain triggers, especially for those folks who have been bullied. I think this book should be recommended reading for young people. This book tackles a big topic - that of bullying. It tells the story from the perspective of a young man who was bullied and the consequences his "abuse" had on his life, and touches on the relationship he had with his family. It tells the story of a strong family relationship, from the perspective of the lawyer who handled the case. While some parts of this book are quite "dry and boring," I think the story in its entirety comes together in the end. As a society, I think we need to do more to stop and somehow learn to prevent bullying and the consequences it can have. It is deep reading for sure. I commend Mr. Bello for tackling such a tough subject. (As a member of Book Sirens, I received a free advance review copy and am leaving this review voluntarily.)</span>

The dialogue going on in Kevin's mind explains the why and how devastating bullying is and what damage it can do to an individual experiencing it.   <span id="freeText4344390854210733322" style="display:none">The cover and title caught attracted me initially and I wanted to read the book. This is a subject that lots of people wonder about. When there are mass shootings in schools the first thing that comes to mind is "WHY"? The dialogue going on in Kevin's mind explains the why and how devastating bullying is and what damage it can do to an individual experiencing it. I loved the character Kenny too, the way he had survived bullying and other traumas but came back to try and stop the shooter becoming the hero instead of a victim. Loved the story and will definitely read other stories from this author.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4344390854210733322" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3619112290" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3619112290" />
    <a title="Arganise Campbell-Nash" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/84155327-arganise-campbell-nash"><img alt="Arganise Campbell-Nash" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3619112290?book_show_action=true">Oct 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arganise Campbell-Nash" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arganise Campbell-Nash" href="/user/show/84155327-arganise-campbell-nash">Arganise Campbell-Nash</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3619112290&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3619112290" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16390943028361135434">Betrayal High by Mark. M. Bello is an engaging thriller about a tragic school shooting at Bloomfield High School that resulted in several lawsuits and a movement for school safety. Kevin Burns planned the day on seeking revenge on his classmates and instructors that contributed to his miserable school experience. He was taunted, bullied, and unloved at home which made him believe he had nothing to lose. Kevin intended to carry out his mission flawlessly, but Kenny Tracey who is the stepson of bi</span>
  <span id="freeText16390943028361135434" style="display:none">Betrayal High by Mark. M. Bello is an engaging thriller about a tragic school shooting at Bloomfield High School that resulted in several lawsuits and a movement for school safety. Kevin Burns planned the day on seeking revenge on his classmates and instructors that contributed to his miserable school experience. He was taunted, bullied, and unloved at home which made him believe he had nothing to lose. Kevin intended to carry out his mission flawlessly, but Kenny Tracey who is the stepson of big-time lawyer Zachary Blake took him down before he could hurt anyone else. A trial begins and the reader starts to see the different personalities of everyone involved in the shooting. Kevin uses his spotlight as a school shooter to shed light on bullying. He implied that if something was done about the cruelty in Bloomfield High School, the nine students would be alive. Kenny was looked at as the hero in the situation. The way he secretly received praised and fan mail reminded me of the way women affectionately cared for Ted Bundy even though he was a murderer.<br /><br /> <br /><br />The prologue was intense, which made me want to read more. The way Burns has the reader dive into the mind of Kevin Burns in a graphic way gave me chills. I was hooked to the book from the very first page. This real-world issue made my imagination run wild creating a number possibilities of how this story could end. Even though this story is fictional, I admired the way Mark M. Bello created this real-world issue into a story that can bring awareness. I was inspired by Kenny and how he used his spotlight as a hero to bring the community together against Bullying and Gun violence. He didn’t allow himself to be a victim, instead, he helped others even Kevin Burns. The characters are well developed so much so that Rolland Barrington instantly became my fictional enemy when I read about dirty dealings in the Black Market.<br /><br /> <br /><br />I would’ve liked more insight from Kenny Tracey’s perspective since he was a major character in the novel. It would’ve helped to read about the change he intended to create from his perspective. I felt that novel focused more on the trials and investigation dealing with gun violence than the activism against bullying. The character development and building towards the plot were in the perfect placement of the story. <br /><br /> <br /><br />Betrayal High is suspenseful, dramatic, and chilling and is recommended for all readers.<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="16390943028361135434" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3613804678" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3613804678" />
    <a title="Sol Tyler" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/111899066-sol-tyler"><img alt="Sol Tyler" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586363569p2/111899066.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3613804678?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sol Tyler" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sol Tyler" href="/user/show/111899066-sol-tyler">Sol Tyler</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3613804678" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1865089530457947725">Wow, what a heart-stopping fifth installment of the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller Series! Trial lawyer, Zachary Blake, has performed some fascinating investigations on the Church and on the death of a black man in Michigan in previous books on this series. This time, he appears on scene again, but to bring relief to families and justice to a whole community which has undergone a terrible bloody episode perpetuated by a young character called Kevin Burns. Tired of being bullied, Burns decides to p</span>
  <span id="freeText1865089530457947725" style="display:none">Wow, what a heart-stopping fifth installment of the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller Series! Trial lawyer, Zachary Blake, has performed some fascinating investigations on the Church and on the death of a black man in Michigan in previous books on this series. This time, he appears on scene again, but to bring relief to families and justice to a whole community which has undergone a terrible bloody episode perpetuated by a young character called Kevin Burns. Tired of being bullied, Burns decides to pull the trigger of his father’s gun at school and leaves everyone asking themselves “why?”. <br />I must admit I love books written in the form of dialogues, and this is actually the way Mark Bello has decided to pen Betrayal High. So, I could not help being hooked right from the very first page. By resorting to such a touchy theme as bullying and by choosing a simple narrative style, Bello has been able to develop a fiction which seems to be a real-life story due to the contemporary content of its thirty four chapters. He has employed the third person singular and has proven that his writing skill is on point. <br />Another important ingredient of this book are the characters. Identifying with the characters is usually one of the reasons why readers love certain books more than others. In this particular case, the main characters and the supporting ones develop like people do in real life and that is one of the reasons why the story is so captivating. <br />Betrayal High is directed to an adult audience, but I believe young adults and adolescents can also enjoy this gem as much as I did. It teaches lessons and allows readers to look at a matter which is, unfortunately, always in vogue from another perspective. <br />Even though this tale belongs to a series, the plot is so well-constructed that it can be read as a standalone. It is definitely an entertaining read that should not be missed! </span>
  <a data-text-id="1865089530457947725" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3614099901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11168721185922522574">This is a breathtaking and thought-provoking novel! “Betrayal High” written by Mark M. Bello is a book that contains thirty-four chapters full of action and tension. <br/><br/>The story takes place in Michigan. It seems like a “normal” high school day for everyone but Kevin Burns, who has been subject of cruel school bullying, has other plans: he is carrying a handgun in one hand, a AK47 over his shoulder and a pressure bomb to take over all the bullies. Kenny Tracey, who is in his senior year, is a good </span>
  <span id="freeText11168721185922522574" style="display:none">This is a breathtaking and thought-provoking novel! “Betrayal High” written by Mark M. Bello is a book that contains thirty-four chapters full of action and tension. <br /><br />The story takes place in Michigan. It seems like a “normal” high school day for everyone but Kevin Burns, who has been subject of cruel school bullying, has other plans: he is carrying a handgun in one hand, a AK47 over his shoulder and a pressure bomb to take over all the bullies. Kenny Tracey, who is in his senior year, is a good and loyal friend and big brother. He had a tough life because his father passed away when he and his brother were little kids. Kenny knows he has to do something, so he tries to take Kevin’s weapons and achieves to stop him. Zachary Blake, Kenny’s step-dad, is a successful lawyer who is convinced to file a lawsuit to everyone involved in this case. Is he going to make it? <br /><br />The suspenseful elements of the plot of this book kept me engaged from the start of the book. Bellos’s writing style is a skill to be appreciated as the sentences are well crafted and enjoyable to read. In fact, he drops significant indicators that keep the suspense alive by referring to a back story. He strings past with present and gives the reader a visual inventory to decipher the tension. <br /><br />I think that the characters are perfectly well-drawn; they are normal people who have been through a lot and that makes it easy to emphasize with them. You can take notice of the mental, spiritual and emotional side of them. <br /><br />All in all, what struck me was the subject of the novel because it is something that happens nowadays all over the world. Teenagers are bullying targets and think that holding guns is the only way to take revenge for themselves. As a primary school teacher I’m very worried about this. I would recommend this book to adults but also to teens because everyone will find something to appreciate. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11168721185922522574" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3557976960" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15775124134725661121">This is Book 5 in the series about Zack Blake, lawyer extraordinaire. In this book, Kenny and Jake, Zack’s stepsons, are headed to school to take final exams. Sadly, a troubled teen, Kevin Burns, who has been bullied at school, decides to take matters in his own hands and takes guns to school, planning to shoot as many students and teachers as he can. After the deadly shooting, Zack is asked to represent the victims against the shooter, the school, and the arms manufacturer, Barrington Arms. Add</span>
  <span id="freeText15775124134725661121" style="display:none">This is Book 5 in the series about Zack Blake, lawyer extraordinaire. In this book, Kenny and Jake, Zack’s stepsons, are headed to school to take final exams. Sadly, a troubled teen, Kevin Burns, who has been bullied at school, decides to take matters in his own hands and takes guns to school, planning to shoot as many students and teachers as he can. After the deadly shooting, Zack is asked to represent the victims against the shooter, the school, and the arms manufacturer, Barrington Arms. Additionally, there is a political bent to this incident, as the US president is heavily connected to Barrington Arms, and he and the US Attorney General want to exact revenge on Zack Blake for retribution for an earlier case. <br />I would have preferred this story to focus on the high school shooting and the families affected by this terrible event. I know that the addition of the political angle is important in light of our current political nightmare, but I thought that took the story off on a tangent. However, having said that, I would love to see the conclusion presented in this book to also play out in our real world, but sadly I don’t think any of the complicit group in congress will step up and do the right thing, as evidenced by the ludicrous handling of the impeachment “trial” in the Senate. So for now, I will have to be content with hoping it were so, and justice served as it is in the novels set forth in the capable hands of Mark M. Bello. <br />#BetrayalHigh #MarkMBello</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('BtXiTSFpv0drQY+eIPCF7+PRzJRocrLYEp4xs0S58EI69aS6iJ8oEq3kspUKltE1u/NUHLyZZX48PAIWVt3KCQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ckG5WuqfTx3qRlxrNFn8hLvKcht+XXY9vDihHpOeYK9OYf+tQ2nYSCzjYWAeP6he4+jqk6q2oZuSmpK7gfpa5A==')})
  }

Above al<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText18445113757039450786\" style=\"display:none\">From the Foreword by Marian Wright EdelmanAfrica’s Child is an unforgettable and searingly personal book….In the face of repeated obstacles and injustices, Nhambu continued to analyze the world around her with wit and a sharp sense of humor. Above all, as a very young child she decided one day that even if there was no other person in the world who loved and wanted her, she was going to love and care for herself—and that decision changed the course of her life. Africa’s Child is the story of a mixed-race girl growing up in the Usambara Mountains of Tanzania, East Africa. Raised in an orphanage with no knowledge of her origins or family, she endured abandonment, hardships, severe illnesses, and bullying. Her experiences as a child and teenager included physical, emotional, and sexual abuse, social stigma, and racial discrimination.Yet Nhambu tells her inspiring story with warmth and humor. Her questioning mind probes the African tribal realities and multi-cultural complexities that impacted her life both at the orphanage and schools run by German nuns as well as at an African high school with American nuns. Nhambu not only survived her childhood but triumphed. Her faith and resilience, along with a belief in learning and her tenacious pursuit of an education, sustained her through many challenges. Dance, especially African tribal dance, became the way she healed and nourished her spirit. Through the love and commitment of an American teacher she met in Africa, Nhambu was able to pursue her dream of education and a new life for herself. The first book in her three-part memoir ends as she is leaving Africa for university studies in America on a full scholarship.Maria Nhambu is the creator of Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout She marries, has two children, and establishes herself in the American way of life. Then a visit to Africa, and especially to Tanzania, reawakens the drumbeats and dancing that she carries in her soul. On her return home, she teaches Swahili and African Studies, performs African dance at schools, and creates Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout based on African dance. She both finds and creates the family she longed for as a child and connects with her unknown background. The first book of the trilogy, Africa’s Child, was released in 2016. Hygge is the feeling you get when you are cuddled up on a sofa with a loved one, in warm knitted socks, in front of the fire, when it is dark, cold and stormy outside. It that feeling when you are sharing good, comfort food with your closest friends, by candle light and exchanging easy conversation. Lagom is the new Scandi lifestyle trend taking the world by storm. This delightfully illustrated book gives you the lowdown on this transformative approach to life and examines how the lagom ethos has helped boost Sweden to the No.10 ranking in 2017\'s World Happiness Report.Lagom (pronounced \'lah-gom\') has no equivalent in the English language but is loosely translated as \'not too little, not too much, just right\'. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6137567094390610868">Mark M. Bello is an attorney, lawsuit finance expert, and award-winning author. A Michigan native, Mark received his B.A. in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree from Thomas M. Cooley Law School.<br/><br/>After years of working high profile legal cases, Mark wanted to provide a front row glimpse of what a victim faces when standing up for justice. Each book in the Zachary Blake Betr</span>
  <span id="freeText6137567094390610868" style="display:none">Mark M. Bello is an attorney, lawsuit finance expert, and award-winning author. A Michigan native, Mark received his B.A. in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree from Thomas M. Cooley Law School.<br /><br />After years of working high profile legal cases, Mark wanted to provide a front row glimpse of what a victim faces when standing up for justice. Each book in the Zachary Blake Betrayal Series is a ripped from the headlines novel inspired by not only Bello’s legal experiences, but his concern for our current sociopolitical landscape. With a creative writing style, he tackles themes of religious freedom, racial and ethnic prejudice, human rights, government influence, and law enforcement.<br /><br />Mark is married and has four adult children and eight grandchildren. In addition to his novels, Mark writes articles/blogs about safety, justice, and fairness in the legal system. His work can be found in numerous print and online publications.<br /><br />Mark is currently working on his fourth novel, set for release in 2019.<br />.<br /><br /> <br /><br />**Visit and follow Mark’s blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.markmbello.com">www.markmbello.com</a><br />**Follow Mark on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/MarkMBelloBooks">www.facebook.com/MarkMBelloBooks</a><br />**Follow Mark on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/MarkMBelloBooks">www.twitter.com/MarkMBelloBooks</a><br />** Follow Mark on Goodreads: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/16283795.Mark_M_Bello">www.goodreads.com/author/show/1628379...</a><br /></span>

But as the Dearborn Police seek to complete their investigation, an organization of white supremacists tries to thwart any attempt to tie their group to the murder and mayhem. Unfortunately, not for long, as a second (and more dangerous) syndicate and its leader plot revenge for their fallen brothers. Their scheme? To steal and release deadly Sarin gas in the city.  Police Captain Jack Dylan and his team are dedicated to thwarting the plot and bringing the culprits to justice. However, with a terrorist threat in play, the FBI usurps the investigation. However, Jack Dylan never backs away from a case or a fight. When the white supremacy leader evades the FBI\'s dragnet, Jack goes rogue and hunts him down in Manistee.  The inevitable standoff finds Dylan alone with his nemesis in an unfamiliar city with no FBI or local law enforcement to support him. His plans go awry, and Jack finds himself arrested by local authorities and placed on trial for his actions.  Attorney Zachary Blake comes to his defense in the biggest trial this quiet community has ever seen. The local cops and the FBI think they have a winner, but Zack and his lead investigator, Micah Love, believe there’s more to the story than meets the eye.  This exciting legal thriller concludes with a dramatic showdown that has become the trademark of award-winning author Mark M.
